%raghu, gv = 105, 013.pdf = 136, 014.pdf = 100

\begin{entry}
\word{sathxla, sathxLa}
\src{kA}
\gl{nA}
\mng{paratatatxvX; adhAyxtamxsAdhakanu tananx BakitxmAgaRdalilx ErabeVkAda muKayx GaTaTx, haMta; idaralilx parxdhAnavAgi Bakatx, maheVsha, parxsAdi, pArxNaliMgi, sharaNa matutx aikayx eMba SaTasxthXlagaLive. ivu aMgasathxla, liMgasathxlagaLeMba eraDu parxkAragaLalilxyU ive. SaTasxthXlagaLalilx parxtiyoMdaralilxyU upaviBAgagaLidudx, avugaLalilx nalavatutxnAlukx aMgasathxlagaLu hAgU aivatetxVLu liMgasathxlagaLU idudx oTuTx nUroMdu muKayxsathxlagaLAgive. manuSayxnalilx sahajavAgiruva guNagaLu, shakitxgaLu, iMdirxyagaLeV muMtAduvu aneVka viBAgagaLAgi I sathxlagaLige saMbaMdhapaDutatxve:}
\expl{sathxlaviDidu savaRdalAyatanAgi sahajaviDidu nijavaLavaTuTxdAgi adideMdenaluMTe (cenanxba. samava. 3-208-678); iMtiV nU\char'273\char'311MTusathxladalilx nipuNanAgi misharxSaDivxdhasathxla SaDusathxla tirxsathxla EkasathxlavAgi sathxla niHsathxlavaneyidx swrASaTxrXsoVmeVshavxraliMga tAnu tAnAgirabeVkayAyx (Adayayx. samava. 6-322-1020); sathxlamoMde tananx shakitxya misukinaMgasathxla liMgasathxlagaLeMderaDAyutx (shUnayxmaM. samava. 11-562-1224).}
\mngnum{paratatatxvX; parabarxhamx:}
\expl{EkaveMdenisida parabarxhamxviralu tAne sathxla (shivaciM. 48-5); anupamasathxlavenalu cinAmxtarxnA liMgavene shivaM tAneyaMgavenelekx jiVvaM (shivaciM. 48-10).}
\mng{sathxLa:}
\explnum{tiLupi jaMgamaliMga BakitxsathxLamanA tirxvidhaparxsAdasathxLamanamaLAcArapadamaM toV{\ri}daDe (basapu. 25-65). manuSayxnalilxruva guNagaLu, iMdirxyagaLu, shakitxgaLu iveV modalAdavugaLalilx aneVka viBAgagaLanunx mADutAtxre. I parxkAramADi avaru avugaLanunx kelavoMdu sathxLakekx saMbaMdhisutAtxre (shivAkoV. 11-17).}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{sathxlakuLa, sathxLakuLa}
\src{kA}
\gl{nA}
\mng{sathxladalilxya viBAgagaLu:}
\expl{vishAvxsada haravariyalilx vishavxmaya sathxlakuLaMgaLAdavu (moVLige. samava. 8-710-2123); mUlava kitatxlilxye halavu baLiLx oNaguvaMte sathxlakuLaMgaLu BinanxBAvavAgi toV{\ru}va iravu a{\ri}talilxyeV naSaTxvAyitutx (bibibxbA. samava. 8-132-355).}
\mngnum{sathxLakuLa:}
\expl{sathxLakuLaMgaLa tiLidu SaDivxdhaliMgagaLalilx dhAyxnapUjAdigaLiMda aMgagoMDu Bavada baTeTxya meTiTxniMdalalxde SaTasxthXlabarxhimxgaLAgaru (akakxma. samava. 5-54-132); sathxLakuLavanetitxdalilx samayakekx dUra cidaCxna BeVda BeVdAMtavanetitxdalilx AdhAyxtamxkekx dUra (koVlashAM. samava. 7-43-92).}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{sathxlajacnx}
\src{kA}
\gl{nA}
\mng{SaTasxthXla, EkoVtatxrashatasathxla muMtAda sathxlagaLa sAravanunx garxhisidavanu:}
\expl{anAcAradalilx AcAravaDagi Bakatxnalalxde BaviyAgi nitayxnalalxde anitayxnAgidadxvaMgalalxde mU{\ru}kuLavilalx
A{\ru}kuLadalilx balalxvanalalxde iMtiva{\rO}LagAda nU{\rO}MdukuLakekx sathxlajacnxnalalx (moVLige. samava. 8-504-1446).}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{sathxlaBeVda}
\src{saM}
\mngnum{eraDu vidha-parabarxhamxsavxrUpi shivatatatxvXdoDane bereta mAyAshakitxya koSxVBeyiMda sathxlavu aMgasathxla matutx liMgasathxla eMdu eraDu vidhavAgutatxde. liMgasathxlavu upAsayx, aMgasathxlavu upAsaka, cinAmxtarxvAda liMgasathxlavu shiva, aMgasathxlavu jiVva.}
\begin{shl}
savxshakitxkoSxVBamAterxVNa sathxlaM tadf divxvidhaM BaveVtf |\\
EkaM liMgasathxlaM porxVkatxmanayxdaMgasathxlaM samxqtamf ||\\
liMgasathxlamupAsayxM sAyxdaMgasathxlamupAsakamf |\\
sathxlaM cinAmxtarxmeVva sAyxlilxMgaM sAyxciCxva Eva hi ||\\
tathAMgaM jiVva Eva sAyxditi sheYviV parA sidhxtiH |
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(a. sU., 2. 10, 13, 18-19)}
\mngnum{Aruvidha liMgasathxlagaLu-liMgasathxlavu modalige iSaTxliMga, pArxNa\-liMga, BAvaliMga eMdu mUru vidhavAgutatxde. I mUru liMgasathxlagaLu matetx talA eraDeraDAgi oTuTx Aru liMgasathxlagaLAgutatxve. avu I riVtiyAgive-iSaTxliMgavu AcAraliMgasathxla, guruliMgasathxlaveMdU; pArxNaliMgavu shivaliMgasathxla, caraliMgasathxlaveMtalU; BAvaliMgavu parxsAda\-liMgasathxla, mahAliMgasathxlaveMdu Aru vidhavAgutatxve.}
\begin{shl}
liMgasathxlaM tirxdhA jecnxVyaM tadeBxVdoV vaNaRyxteV karxmAtf |\\
parxthamaM BAvaliMgaM sAyxdf divxtiVyaM pArxNaliMgakamf ||\\
taqtiVyamiSaTxliMgaM sAyxdeyxVtatf tirxvidhaM samxqqtamf |\\
mahAliMgaM parxsAdAKayxM liMgamituyxBayasathxlamf ||\\
BAvaliMgaM BavateyxVva sAvxnuBUti parxmANataH |\\
tathA ca caraliMgaM ca shivaliMgamiti davxyamf ||\\
pArxNaliMgaM BavateyxVva sAvxnuBUtiparxmANataH |\\
guruliMgaM tathA{\char'263}cAraliMgamituyxBayasathxlamf |\\
iSaTxliMgaM BavateyxVva satayxmukatxmidaM mayA ||
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(a. sU., 3. 5-6, 17-20; caM. A., kirx. pA., 3. 23, 26-27)}
\mngnum{Aru vidha aMgasathxlagaLu-aMgasathxlavu tAyxgAMga, BoVgAMga, yoVgAMgaveMdu mUru vidha. I mUru matetx talA eraDeraDu sathxlagaLAgi oTuTx Aru sathxlagaLAgutatxve. avu hiVgive-tAyxgAMgavu Bakatxsathxla, mAheVshavxrasathxla eMdU; BoVgAMgavu parxsAdisathxla, pArxNaliMgisathxla eMdU; yoVgAMgavu sharaNasathxla, aikayxsathxla eMdu oTuTx Aru sathxlagaLAgutatxve.}
\begin{shl}
aMgasathxlaM tirxdhA jecnxVyamAcAyeRYH sUkaSxmXdashiRBiH |\\
yoVgAMgaM parxthamaM porxVkatxM BoVgAMgaM tu divxtiVyakamf ||\\
tayxgAMgaM tu taqtiVyaM sAyxdeVvameVva tirxdhA BaveVtf ||\\
yoVgAMgameYkayxM sharaNasathxla mituyxBayaM BaveVtf |\\
pArxNaliMgiparxsAdiVti davxyaM BoVgAMgamiSayxteV ||\\
mAheVshavxrasathxlaM Bakatxsathxla mituyxBayaM tathA |\\
tAyxgAMgaM BavatiVteyxVvaM porxVcayxteV pAramAthiRkeYH ||
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(a. sU., 4. 5-6, 12-13)}
\mngnum{ipapxtetxVLu vidha-anAdi viVrasheYva sArasaMgarxhadalilx beVroMdu karxmadiMda ipapxtetxVLu sathxlagaLanunx nirUpisalAgide. avugaLu I riVtiyAgive-(1) piVThikAsUtarxsathxla, (2) anAdiBakatxlakaSxNasathxla, (3) AdirahitajaMgamasathxla, (4) shUnayxliMgasathxla, (5) niSakxlaliMgasathxla, (6) mahAliMgasathxla, (7) parxNavAkaqtiliMgasathxla, (8) vishavxjananasathxla. (9) piMDasathxla, (10) piMDacitfsathxla, (11) saMsAraheVyaBAgasathxla, (12) gurukAruNayxsathxla, (13) liMgadhAraNasathxla, (14) deVshikamahatatxvXsathxla, (15) sevxVSaTxliMgamAhAtamxyXsathxla, (16) caraliMgamAhAtamxyXsathxla, (17) parxsAdamAhAtamxyXsathxla, (18) pAdoVdakamahatatxvXsathxla, (19) BasamxmAhAtamxyX sathxla, (20) rudArxkaSx mahatatxvX sathxla, (21) paMcAkaSxra mahatatxvX sathxla, (22) Bakatxsathxla, (23) mAheVshavxrasathxla, (24) parxsAdisathxla, (25) pArxNaliMgisathxla, (26) sharaNasathxla, (27) aikayxsathxla.}
\begin{shl}
athAtashAcxnAdi viVrasheYvasArasusaMgarxheV |\\
sathxlAnayxtarx nigadayxMteV sapatxviMshatiBeVdataH ||\\

................... ||\\
sharaNasathxlameYkayxsayx sathxlaM sAyxtf sapatxviMshatiH || 
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(a. viV. sA. saM., 1. 47-58)}
\mngnum{mUvatAtxru vidha-AcAraliMgasathxla modalAda Aru liMgasathxlagaLalilx parxtiyoMdu sathxlavU moVhi, Bakatx, pUjaka, viVra, parxsAdi, pArxNi eMdu Aru vidhavAgi oTuTx mUvatAtxru sathxlagaLAgutatxve.}
\begin{shl}

\end{shl}

\begin{entry}
\word{sathxlaleVpa}
\src{va}
\mng{sAdhakanu tananx guriyanunx inUnx muTaTxdeV iruvAga tananx AdhAyxtimxka dAriyanunx Bakatxsathxla, maheVshavxrasathxla, itAyxdiyAgi viMgaDisutAtxne. Adare aikayxsathxlavanunx sAdhisida meVle sAdhaka sAdhayx sididhx ivugaLa vayxtAyxsa ilalxvAgi sathxla mUvatAtxrU iruvudilalx, ArU iruvudilalx, aMgasathxla liMgasathxla eMba eraDu sathxlagaLU iruvudilalx. Aga iruvudelAlx oMdeV sathxla. aikayxnAdavanu A oMdeV sathxlavanunx tananx jiVvanada parxti aMgakUkx leVpisikoMDirutAtxne. (8:2005).}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{sapxshaRnoVdaka}
\src{kA}
\gl{nA}
\mngnum{dashavidhapAdoVdakagaLalilx oMdu; (kirxyAdaqSiTxganuguNavAgi) tananx beraLugaLiMda nAlageya meVliTuTxkoMDaMtaha pAdoVdaka:}

\mngnum{jaMgamara pAdagaLanunx tananx keYgaLiMda muTuTxvudu:}
\expl{kirxyApAdoVdaka mADabeVkAdaDe ...tananx hasatxdiMda pAdava muTiTx mADidaMtahade sapxshaRnoVdakavenisuvudu (cenanxba. samava. 3-599-1631); savxya cara para guru caramUtiRgaLa apiRtAvadhAnava nilukaDeyeMteMdaDe ...hasatxviTuTx sapxshaRnava mADe sapxshaRnoVdakavenisuvadayayx (sidadhxrA. samava. 4-51). tAtivxka daqSiTxyiMda keLage heVLidaMte ivugaLanunx vivarisabahudAgide ...catudaRLa vikasitavAgalu sapxshaRnoVdakavu (shivAkoV. 104-141).}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{samxrAri}
\src{saM}
\mng{maKAri, kAlAri, purAri, samxrAri, veVdAri eMba aidu vidha paMcamaralilx (viVrasheYva Bakatxralilx) obabx. samxrAriyu shirxV sheYlapiVThada BakatxnAgidudx, vaqSaBagoVtarx. mUlaguru paMDitArAdhayx, sUtarx mukAtxgucaCx, sUthxlapaMcAkaSxriV maMtarx (OM hArxM hirxVM namaH shivAya).}

\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{savxsitxkAroVhaNa diVkeSx}
\src{va}
\mng{saMsAravanunx heVyavAgi kaMDu, liMgAMga sAmarasayxvanunx paDeyabeVkeMba iceCxyiMda baMda shiSayxnige guruvu koDuva aneVka vidhada diVkeSxgaLalilx idu modalaneyadu. modalu hAlu, tupapx, bALehaNuNx, kabubx matutx jeVnutupapx ivugaLanonxLagoMDa paMcAmaqtadiMda shiSayxnige aBiSeVka mADisi, sharaNa gaNagaLu hasotxVdaka, maMtorxVdaka, shudodhxVdaka, gaMdhoVdaka matutx puSopxVdaka eMba paMcoVdakagaLiMda avanige sAnxnamADisutAtxre. mUraMgula udadxvAda daBeRyanunx toVrisi, tirxvidha maMtarx samxraNeyiMda, adanunx avana soMTakekx kaTuTxtAtxre, ariSaDavxgaRgaLanunx gelulx eMdu boVdhisi, bALe giDada paTeTxyanunx kwpiVnadaMte (SaDakaSxra maMtarx heVLutAtx) kaTuTxtAtxre. suLuLx heVLabeVDa, satayxvanenxV nuDi, koDuva tegedukoLuLxva vicAradalilx ApatxtavxdiMda naDeduko, eMdu heVLi guruvu, alilxruva sharaNagaNagaLa opipxge paDedu, shiSayxna masatxkada meVle hasatxvaninxDutAtxne, hAgU alilx guru shiSayx BeVdaBAvavaLidu guruvu shiSayxna sUtarxvanUnx, shiSayxnu guruvina sUtarxvanUnx hiDiyutAtxre. alilxruva BaqtayxriMda kaLasAcaRne racisi, parxmathagaNa, ArAdhayx, Bakatx, mAheVshavxraroDagUDi, navaratanxKacitavAda shUnayxsiMhAsanada meVle, maMtarxveV mUtiRgoMDiruvaMte kuLitiruva niraMjana jaMgamakekx viBUti, viVLayx, suvaNaR, dashAMGanasAra, puSapxmAle, vasAtxrXBaraNa eMba sapatxpadAthaRgaLanunx koDuvaMtahudeV savxsitxkAroVhaNa diVkeSx (10:687).}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{sAdAKayx}
\src{saM}
\mng{biMdu-nAdarUpagaLuLaLx parAshakitx-Adishakitxyara samAgamadiMda utapxtitxyAguva jagatitxna saqSiTxge kAraNavAguva shivatatatxvX. satf-citf-AnaMda savxrUpiyU, niguRNa parameVshavxranu pUjayx-pUjakaBAvadiMda saguNanAgalu sAdAKayx modalAda parxBeVdavanunx paDeyutAtxne. sAdAKayxvu shiva\-sAdAKayx, amUtaRsAdAKayx, mUtaRsAdAKayx, kataqRsAdAKayx, kamaRsAdAKayx eMdu aidu vidha. I paMca sAdAKayxgaLu sadAshiva, Isha, barxhamx, Ishavxra, IshAna eMba hesarugaLiMda kareyalapxTiTxve.}
\begin{shl}
shivasutx sacicxdAnaMdalakaSxNaH parameVshavxraH |\\
pUjayxpUjakaBAveVna niguRNaH saguNoV BaveVtf ||\\

sadAshiveVshabarxhemxVsha IshavxreVshAnaBeVdataH |\\
mUtaRyoV veY mahAdeVvi sAdAKAyxparanAmakAH || 
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(sU. A., kirx. pA., 1. 23-26; 1. 31-37)}

\src{va}
\mng{`sAdAKayx' eMba padavu `satf' (`nijavAda') `AKayx' (`muKa') eMba padagaLiMda kUDi Adudu. A saMsakxqqta padakekx muKa matutx bAyi eMba eraDu athaRgaLidudx vacanakAraru I padavanunx eraDU athaRgaLalilx baLasutAtxre.}\\
\imng{sAdAKayxgaLu AreMdu kelavu vacanakAraru, aideMdu kelavu vacanakAraru aBipArxyapaDutAtxre. aSeTx alalx, sAdAKayxgaLa savxrUpa matutx kataRvayxgaLa bagegU omamxtavilalx. toVMTada sidadhxliMga shivayoVgigaLeV sAdAKayxgaLu aideMdu kelavu sAri heVLi, AreMdu kelavu sAri heVLutAtxre. udAharaNege noVDi 11:36, 63, itAyxdi.}\\
\imng{sAdAKayxgaLa hesarugaLU saha oMdeV teraniruvudilalx. toVMTada sidadhx\-liMga shivayoVgigaLu mahAsAdAKayx, shivasAdAKayx, mUtiRsAdAKayx, amUtiRsAdAKayx, kataqRsAdAKayx matutx kamaRsAdAKayx eMba Aru sAdAKayxgaLanunx gurutisidAdxre. (11:63) kelavaru sAdAKayxgaLige sadoyxVjAta, vAmadeVva, aGoVra, tatupxruSa matutx IshAna eMba hesarugaLanunx koTiTxdAdxre.}\\
\imng{AgamagaLalilxyU, vacanagaLalilxyU baruva I padakekx pArxyashaH I athaRvididxVtu: shivanu citfsavxrUpanAdudariMda avanu iMdirxyAtiVta matutx manoVtiVta. aMtha shivanu Bakatxrige kANisikoLaLxbeVkAdare yAvudAdaroMdu \hbox{mAdhayxma} beVku, athavA avanu yAvudAdaroMdu rUpadalilx parxkAshisabeVku. iMtha mAdhayxma athavA parxkAshaveV muKa athavA sAdAKayx. athARtf, parashivanu shakitxgaLanunx cinamxya mADuva mUlaka parxkAshisutAtxne (vayxkatxvAgu)tAtxne. hiVge shivanu obabxneV AdarU Bakatxrige aidu (athavA Aru) rUpagaLalilx kANisikoLuLxtAtxne. Adare A muKagaLu iMdirxyagoVcaravalalx.}\\
\imng{sAdAKayx parikalapxneyu pArxyashaH parashivana savaRvAyxpakatavxvanUnx savaRjacnxtavxvanUnx parxtibiMbisutatxve. heVgeMdare: kAladeVshagaLa mitigoLapaTaTx mAnavanu yAvudAdaroMdu sathxLa athavA dikikxge hoVgabalalxnu, Adare para\-shivanu elAlx Aru dikukxgaLigU (meVle, keLage, hiMde, muMde, eDa matutx bala) EkakAlakekx hoVgabalalxnu. athavA vAyxpisikoLaLxbalalxnu. adeV riVti manuSayxnu oMdu kAladalilx oMdeV dikikxnalilx noVDabalalxnu, athavA noVDi ariyabalalxnu. Adare parashivanu Aru dikukxgaLalilx EkakAladalilx noVDi tiLiyabalalxnu. hiVge noVDalu avanige Aru muKagaLu beVku. A daqSiTx\-yiMda parashivanige Aru sAdAKayxgaLive eMdu vacanakAraru heVLirabahudu. kelavu sAri nAlukx dikukxgaLanunx noVDalu nAlukx muKagaLU, madhayxdalilxralU aidaneV muKavU beVkeMdu kelavaru aideV sAdAKayxgaLu sAkeMdu naMbirabahudu.}\\
\imng{meVlina I eraDu athaRgaLu keVvala Uheya AdhArada meVle niMtidudx, avugaLa bagege vacanakAraru Enu heVLutAtxreMbudanunx noVDoVNa. avaru saqSiTxge saMbaMdhisidaMte paMcasAdAKayx kalapxneyanunx hiVge parxtipAdisidAdxre. mUlashakitxyu parashivanalilx yAvAgalU avinABAvadiMda irutatxde. adu parxLayakAladalilx avanalilx avayxkatxvAgi aDagidadxre, saqSiTxya kAladalilx vayxkatxvAgutatxde. Adare avayxkatxvAgidadx shakitxyu nAnA haMtagaLalilx vikasitavAgi, konege parxpaMcada vividha carAcaravasutxgaLAgi vayxkatxvAgabeVkAdare, adakekx parxti haMtadalilxyU perxVraNe matutx mAgaRdashaRna niVDi, adanunx niyaMtirxsalu parashivaneMba cidavxsutx beVkeV beVku. vividha haMtagaLalilx vikasitavAda shakitxge parashakitx, Adishakitx, muMtAda hesarugaLiruvaMte, avugaLige vividha haMtagaLalilx perxVraNe matutx mAgaRdashaRna niVDuva parashivanigU shivasAdAKayx, amUtiRsAdAKayx muMtAda hesarugaLive. vacanakAraru yAva sAdAKayx yAva shakitxya jotegirutatxde eMbudanunx hiVge tiLisidAdxre.}\\
\imng{sadoyxVjAta athavA shivasAdAKayx -- shAMtayxtiVta kale athavA parAshakitx}\\
\imng{vAmadeVva athavA amUtiRsAdAKayx -- shAMtikalA athavA Adi\-shakitx}\\
\imng{aGoVra athavA mUtiRsAdAKayx -- vidAyxkalA athavA icACxshakitx}\\
\imng{tatupxruSa athavA kataqRsAdAKayx -- parxtiSAThxkalA athavA jAcnxnashakitx}\\
\imng{IshAnayx athavA kamaRsAdAKayx -- nivaqtitxkalA athavA kirxyAshakitx}\\
\imng{shiva tAnobabxneV saqSiTxsalAra, shakitx tAnoMdeV vikAsavAgalAradu. shivana perxVraNeyaMte shakitx vikAsavAdare adeV saqSiTx.}\\
\imng{AdhAyxtimxka jiVvanada daqSiTxyiMda noVDidAga, sAdAKayx parikalapxnege hecicxna athaR barutatxde. Aga `sAdAKayx'kekx bAyi eMbathaR koDabeVkAgutatxde. Bakatxnu iDiV vishavxvU tananx deVha, iMdirxya, karaNAdigaLelalxvU shivaniMda paDeda sAlaveMdu tiLidu, avugaLanunx hiMdirugisuvudu tananx kataRvayxveMdu tiVmARnisidAga, avana nijavAda AdhAyxtimxka jiVvana pArxraMBavAgutatxde. Aga avanu tananx elalxvanUnx aMdare, tAnu seVvisuva niVru, AhAra, keVLuva shabadx, vAsisuva vAsane, budidhxVMdirxya kameRVMdirxyagaLu modalAdavugaLelalxvanUnx parashivanige samapiRsutAtxne. hiVge samapiRsuvAga avanu AyA padAthaRgaLanunx keYyalilx sapxshiRsadeV, avelilxyoV alilxMdaleV, manasisxnalelxV, parashivana Aru athavA aidu bAyigaLige (sAdAKayxgaLige) apiRsutAtxne. A mAtu ``... ininxdakekx apiRta muKaMgaLa heVLihenu: guruliMga, shivaliMga, jaMgamaliMga, parxsAdaliMga, mahAliMga I aidu liMgavU AcAraliMgakekx muKaveMdariyalubeVkayAyx. shivaliMga, jaMgamaliMga, parxsAdaliMga, mahAliMga, AcAraliMga I aidu liMgavu guruliMgakekx muKaveMdu ariyalu beVkayAyx...hiVMge aMgamuKagaLalilxyU liMgaveV muKavAgipapx BeVdavanariyabeVkayAyx...'' (11:413) eMba toVMTada sidadhxliMga shiva\-yoVgigaLa vacanadiMda sapxSaTxvAgutatxde. Aga namamx iMdirxyada parxti\-yoMdu bAgilu liMgada parashivana bAyiyAgutatxde. I mAtU saha ``aMgavAda Bakatxnu sucitatxveMba hasatxdiMda AcAraliMgakekx  GArxNaveMba muKadalilx gaMdhada samapaRNava mADi AcAraliMgada parxsananx parxsAdava sivxVkarisutitxpapxnayAyx. jalaveV aMgavAda maheVshavxranu subudidhxyeMba hasatxdiMda guruliMgakekx jihevxyeMba muKadalilx rasavanu samapaRNava mADi guruliMgada parxsananx parxsAdava sivxVkarisutitxpapxnayAyx...'' (11:414) eMba avara vacanadiMdaleV sapxSaTxvAgutatxde.}\\
\imng{kelavu saqSiTxya vacanagaLalilx shakitxvikAsada parikalapxneya jotege sAdAKayxda parikalapxneyU barutatxde. alilxyU saha sAdAKayx eMba padakekx bAyi eMbathaRveV ide. udAharaNege A ... A ``liMgada madhayxdalilx biVjadiMda vaqkaSxvu udayavAguva hAMge, A liMgavu tananx icACxshakitxya kUDikoMDu jagadutapxtitx sithxti layaMgaLige katuRvAgi... opupxtitxpupxdu sadAshivamUtiR. A sadAshivana IshAnayxmuKadalilx AkAsha puTiTxtutx, tatupxruSamuKadalilx vAyu puTiTxtutx..."  (11:67) eMba vacanavU, ``iMteneva shivana muKadalilx ogeda BUtagaLAvuveMdaDe: sadoyxVjAta muKadalilx paqthivx, vAmadeVva muKadalilx apupx, aGoVra muKadalilx aginx, tatupxruSa muKadalilx vAyu, IshAnayx muKadalilx AkAsha" (11:545) eMba vacanavU I mAtanunx puSiTxVkarisutatxde. hiVge sAdAKayxgaLu heVge shivana saqSiTxyoV hAgeyeV, sAdAKayxgaLu shakitxyoDagUDi vividha tatavxgaLanunx saqSiTxsutatxve.}\\
\imng{ililx bAyi athavA muKa eMba athaRvu `parashivanige vAsatxvavAgiyU oMdu deVhavide, adakokxMdu taleyide, adaralolxMdu bAyiyide' eMba tapupx kalapxnege eDemADikoDabAradu. aneVka dAshaRnika vicAragaLanunx nAvu neVravAda BASeyalilx heVLalu sAdhayxvilalx. Agelalx nAvu upame muMtAda AlaMkArika BASeyanenxV baLasuvudu anivAyaRvAgutatxde. parashivana muKa, sAdAKayx, iMdirxyagaLa bAgilu, vishavxtoVbAhu, suhasatx, muMtAda padagaLU aMtaha itara padagaLU AlaMkArika BASeyeV. avugaLanunx vAcAyxthaRdalilx tegedukoLaLxbAradu. hAge vAcAyxthaRdalilx tegedukoMDare shivanige mAnavaguNagaLanunx AroVpisabeVkAgutatxde. shivanige aSaTxtanu (paqthivx, jala, aginx, vAyu, AkAsha, Atamx sUyaR matutx caMdarx eMba eMTu GaTakagaLiMda kUDida deVha) ide eMdu toVMTada sidadhxliMga shivayoVgigaLU itara vacanakArarU heVLidarU, A aSaTxtanu namamx tanuvinaMtahudalalx eMdu avareV heVLutAtxre. udAharaNege ``AkAravilalxdAtaMge aMgaveMdeVke kalipxsi heVLuviri?" eMdu sidadhxliMga shivayoVgigaLu keVLuvAga, parashivanige namamx AkArada deVhavilalx eMba avara aBipArxya sapxSaTxvAgutatxde.}

\word{sAthxvaraliMga}
\src{saM}
\mng{BUmiya meVle parxtiSAThxpisida shivaliMga. viVrasheYvaru sAthxvaraliMgagaLa nimARlAyxdigaLanunx sivxVkarisabAradeMba niyamavide.}
\begin{shl}
na hi sAthxvaraliMgAnAM nimARlAyxduyxpayujayxteV |
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(si. shi., 9. 33)}
\SEE{sAthxvara}

\src{va}
\mng{vacanakAraru idanunx eraDu athaRgaLalilx baLasidAdxre.}\\
\imng{1. sithxravAda athavA calisada liMga. guDiyalilx athavA maTha athavA manegaLalilx parxtiSAThxpitavAgiruva liMgagaLelalx sAthxvaraliMgagaLeV. I athaRdalilx sAthxvaraliMgavu iMdirxyagoVcara, kalilxnalilx mADida oMdu vishiSaTx AkAra matutx gAtarxda liMga. idu sAMparxdAyika hiMdUgaLa parxkAra, parashivana parxtiVkavAdarU, vacanakAraru sAthxvaraliMga pUjeyanunx kaTuvAgi KaMDisidAdxre.}\\
\imng{2. liMga (parashiva) yAvAgalU sAthxvaraveV (acalaveV). iruvudelalx parashivaneV AgiruvudariMdalU, elelxlilxyU avaneV iruvudariMdalU avanu calisutAtxneMdu kalipxsikoLaLxlU sAdhayxvilalx. avanu calisutAtxneMdu kalipxsikoLaLxbeVkAdare, avaniruva matutx avanilalxda sathxLagaLanunx modalu kalipxsikoMDu, avaniruva sathxLadiMda, Igilalxda sathxLakekx calisutitxdAdxneMdu kalipxsikoLaLxbeVkAgutatxde. Adare avanilalxda sathxLaveV ilalxveMda meVle, avanu calisalu sAdhayxveV ilalx. Aga avanu sAthxvara mAtarx, basavaNaNxnavaru sAthxvara jaMgama oMdeV (1:187) eMdu heVLuvAga, tirugADuva liMgavAda jaMgamanU, sAthxvaranAda parashivanU oMdeV horatu, beVrebeVreyalalx eMbathaR avara mAtigide. hAgeyeV `jaMgamakekxredare sAthxvara neneyitutx' eMdAgalU, jaMgamanige eredare, parashiva nenedaMte eMbathaRvAgutatxde.}

\src{kA}
\gl{nA}
\mng{= sAthxvara:}
\expl{aMgada meVle liMgasAhitayxvAda baLika sAthxvaraliMgakekx{\ra}galAgadu (cenanxba. samava. 3-264-867); aMgada meVle liMgadeVvanidadxMte itara sAthxvaraliMgakekx hoVgi hoVgi deVvara kaMDeneMdu nalidu ulivutitxpapx sale manujarugaLige upadeVshava mADuva guruviMge puNayxda baTeTxya koDa (urideV. samava. 6-393-1218).}
\end{entry}

\mng{liMgadhAraNacaMdirxkAkArarAda shirxV niVlakaMTha shivAcAyaRra aBipArxyadalilx pUjAdi kAyaRgaLalilx sUtakagaLu ilalxdiruvaMte, beVre saMdaBaRgaLalilxyU viVrasheYvarige sUtakavilalxde parishudadhxrAgirutAtxre. heVgeMdare aginxya saMpakaRvanunx paDeda kabibxNavu sAmAnayx kabibxNavAgadiruvaMte, aMgada meVlina liMgasaMpakaRdiMda manuSayxru pArxkaqtarAguvudilalx. eNeNxya saMpakaRvanunx paDeda hatitxyu diVpada saMpakaRdiMda diVpaveV AguvaMte sadaBxkitxyiMda kUDida iSaTxliMgada saMpakaRdiMda mAnavanu liMgaveV AgutAtxne. athARtf viVrasheYvarige yAvudeV riVtiya sUtakagaLa doVSaviruvudilalx.}

\begin{entry}
\word{sUtaka nAlukx}
\src{va}
\mng{}\\
\mng{1. shabadxsUtaki: tamage elAlx gotutx eMdu heVLikoLuLxva ajAcnxnigaLu (3:653).}\\
\imng{2. liMgasUtaki: mAtumAtige liMgavenunxva Adare liMgada mahatavx gotitxlalxdavanu (3:676).}\\
\imng{3. jaMgamasUtaki: nijavAda jaMgama yAru eMdu tiLiyadeyeV mAtumAtige jaMgama jaMgama enunxvavanu.}\\

\end{entry}

parxsAdoV{\char'263}sayx parAnaMdaparxkAshaH parikiVtayxRteV ||\\
seVvoyxV guruH samxqqtoV hayxsayx parxsAdoV{\char'263}nuBavoV mataH |\\
tadeVkAveVsharUpeVNa tadAvxnf seVvayxparxsAdavAnf ||
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(si. shi., 18. 71-72)}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{seVvayxparxsAdi}
\src{kA}
\gl{nA}
\mngnum{= seVvayxparxsAdisathxla:}
\expl{parxsAdaliMgatirxvidha AdiparxsAdi aMtayxparxsAdi seVvayxparxsAdi (cenanxba. samava. 3-255-849); iSaTxliMgavanunx soVMki baMda parxsAdavu pArxNaliMgavanunx soVMki, Aga uMTAda parxsAdavanunx sivxVkarisalu adu seVvayxparxsAdiyu (shivAkoV. 110-156).}
\mngnum{jaMgamaparxsAdavanunx sivxVkarisuvavanu:}
\expl{parxsAdaliMgatirxvidha -ivu AdiparxsAdi, aMtayxparxsAdi, seVvayxparxsAdi eMdu ive ...jaMgamamuKadiMda taqpitxyanunx anuBavisidalilx seVvayxparxsAdiyu ivanu mAyAparxpaMcavanunx aLidavanu (shivAkoV. 90-106).}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{hasatxgaLu (suhasatxgaLu)}
\src{va}
\mng{AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya parxthama haMtadalilx sAdhakanu AhAravanunx liMgakekx tananx keYyiMda neYveVdayx (apaRNe) mADutAtxne. Adare jagatutx, jiVva matutx parashiva ivara bagegina tananx jAcnxna hecAcxdaMtelAlx keVvala tinunxva AhAra padAthaRgaLananxSeTxV alalx, itara `AhAra'gaLanUnx avanu apiRsalu pArxraMBisutAtxne. rUpa, rasa, gaMdha, sapxshaRna matutx shabadx ivu karxmavAgi kaNuNx, nAlage, mUgu, camaR matutx kivigaLa AhAragaLu (viSayagaLu). Adare tinunxva AhAravanunx keYyiMda apiRsuvaMte uLida AhAragaLanunx (aiMdirxka viSayagaLanunx) keYyiMda apiRsalu baruvudilalx. Alalxde, tinunxva AhAravanunx avanu oMdu nidiRSaTx samayadalilx matutx oMdu nidiRSaTx sathxLadalilx apiRsutAtxne. Adare iMdirxyaviSayagaLige I kAladeVshagaLa mitiyilalx. Bakatxnu avugaLanunx avu elilxveyo alilxMdale, aMtaHkaraNadalelxV apiRsutAtxne. hiVge avana aMtaHkaraNa catuSaTxyavu sAMkeVtikavAgi athavA AlaMkArikahasatxvenisikoLuLxtatxve. Aru liMgagaLige Aru haMtada sAdhakanu yAvAva `AhAra'vanunx yAvAva suhasatxdiMda apiRsutAtxne eMbudakekx vivara hiVgide:}\\
\imng{1. sAdhakanu BakatxsathxladalilxruvAga tananx paMcaBUtagaLalolxMdAda paqthivxVtatavxdalilxruva sugaMdhavanunx sadaBxkitx (sharxdAdhxBakitx)yiMda sucitatx hasatxdiMda AcAra\-liMgakekx apiRsutAtxne. sucitatxvu sAdhAraNa citatxda AdhAyxtimxkavAgi sudhArita rUpa. sAdhAraNa janara citatxvu tamamx hiMdina janamxda vAsanegaLiMda matutx anAdiyAgi baMda mareviniMdAgi Enelalx vasutxgaLige Ase paDutitxdadxre, sAdha\-kana sucitatxvu tananx elalx AsegaLanUnx parashivanigeV apiRsutatxde.}\\
\imng{2. maheVshasathxladalilxruva sAdhakanu jalatatavxdalilxruva surasavanunx neYSiThxkA\-BakitxyiMda subudidhx eMba hasatxdiMda guruliMgakekx apiRsutAtxne. subudidhxyu sAdhAraNa budidhxya AdhAyxtimxka rUpa. sAdhAraNa janara budidhx kelavu vasutxgaLanunx oLeLxyaveMdU, kelavanunx keTaTxveMdU nidhaRrisidare, subudidhxyu A BeVdavanenxV shivanigapiRsi suKaduHKa, hogaLike-tegaLikegaLanunx samAna budidhxyiMda noVDutatxde.}\\
\imng{3. parxsAdiyu aginxtatavxdalilxruva surUpanunx avadhAnaBakitxyiMda nirahaMkArahasatxdiMda shivaliMgakekx apiRsutAtxne. nijavAda parxsAdiyu tananx anuBavakekx baMda vasutxgaLanunx oLeLxyavu keTaTxvu eMba BeVdaBAvadiMda noVDade, yAvudanUnx devxVSisade hAgU tirasakxrisade, yAvudanUnx iSaTxpaDade, elalxvanUnx apiRsi parxsAdavanAnxgi mADikoMDidAdxne.}\\ 
\imng{4. pArxNaliMgiyu vAyutatavxdalilxruva susapxshaRnavanunx anuBAva Bakitx\-yiMda sumanahasatxdiMda jaMgamaliMgakekx apiRsutAtxne. elalxvanUnx shivaneV nidhaRrisutAtxneMdU, idaralilx garxhagatigaLa pAtarxveVnU ilalxveMdU avanu naMbiruvudariMda avanu joyxVtiSayxshAsatxrXvanunx naMbuvudilalx; anayxdhamaR, anayxyoVgagaLanunx avanu naMbuvudilalx.}\\
\imng{5. sharaNasathxladalilxruva sAdhakanu AkAshatatavxdalilxruva sushabadxvanunx AnaMda\-BakitxyiMda sujAcnxnahasatxdiMda parxsAdaliMgakekx apiRsutAtxne. avanu jagatetxlalx shivamayaveMdu parigaNisuvudariMda, tAnu keVLuva shabadxvelalxvU sushabadxveMdeV tiLiyutAtxne. EkeMdare, shivApiRtavAda elalx shabadxgaLU sushabadxvAgeV parivatiRtavAgabeVku. alalxde avanu AdaSuTx shivana bagegina japa, Bajane, vacana, kathegaLanunx mAtarx keVLaliciCxsutAtxne.}\\
\imng{6. aikayxnu Atamxdalilxruva elalx iMdirxyagaLa pariNAmavanunx (taqpitxyanunx) samarasaBakitxyiMda sadABxvahasatxdiMda mahAliMgakekx apiRsutAtxne. sujAcnxnahasatxvu iMdirxyaviSayagaLanunx iSaTxliMgada seVvakaranAnxgiyU, paMcavAyugaLanunx pArxNaliMgada seVvakaranAnxgiyU, avasAthxtarxyagaLanunx BAva\-liMgada seVvakaranAnxgiyU mADutatxde.}\\
\imng{kelavu veVLe, vacanakAraru `hasatx' eMba padada `suhasatx' eMba padavanunx baLasutAtxre.}\\
\imng{kelavu vacanakAraru I sUkaSxmX athavA AdhAyxtimxka hasatxgaLu oMbatetxMdu heVLi, uLida mUru hasatxgaLa kAyaRgaLanunx I riVti vivarisidAdxre.}\\
\imng{7. ninARma hasatx: aSATxvaraNa matutx paMcAcAragaLanunx tapapxde AcarisuvaMte parxcoVdisuva hasatx. tanagAgi EnanUnx mADade (tananx hesaranenxV maretu) elalxvanUnx shivanigeV mADabeVkeMba hasatx.}\\
\imng{8. niSakxLaMka hasatx: viVrasheYva dhamaRda elalx AcAragaLanUnx tapapxdaMte AcarisuvaMte parxcoVdisuva hasatx.}\\
\imng{9. nirALa hasatx: sAdhakanu tananxnenx saMpUNaRvAgi parashivanige apiRsuva hasatx.}\\
\imng{I oMbatutx hasatxgaLalilx modalina Arara vicAravu SaTfsathxla sidAdhxMtakakxnuguNavAgidudx athaRpUNaRvAgide. uLida mUru hasatxgaLa vicAravu athaRvAgadaMtidudx, anAvashayxkavenisutatxde.}
\end{entry}
